]

# Students who submitted presentations (from email subjects)
submitted_ids = [
    "1800016633", "1800090104", "1800093002", "1900016620", "1900016628",
    "2000012117", "2000012969", "2000014178", "2000014180", "2000016605",
    "2000016606", "2100016613"
]

# Find students who haven't submitted
missing_students = [student for student in students if student["id"] not in submitted_ids]

print(f"Total students in course: {len(students)}")
print(f"Students who submitted: {len(submitted_ids)}")
print(f"Students missing submissions: {len(missing_students)}")
print("\nMissing students:")
for student in missing_students:
    print(f"- {student['name']} (ID: {student['id']}, Email: {student['email']})") code
